[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m: * final InputStream is = [0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35minput.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:     * Constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@value[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m used to identify the PACK200 compression [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m118[0m[39m:     *[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m119[0m[39m:     * @since [0m[1;36m1.3[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/CompressorStreamFactory.jav[0m[1;92ma:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m431[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m439[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m431[0m[39m:    private final int memoryLimitInKb;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m432[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m433[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m434[0m[39m:     * Constructs an instance with the decompress Concatenated option set to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m435[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m436[0m[39m:    public [0m[1;35mCompressorStreamFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m437[0m[39m:        this.decompressUntilEof = null;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m438[0m[39m:        this.memoryLimitInKb = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m439[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:81[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        blockMode = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthirdByte & BLOCK_MODE_MASK[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:        maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockMode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35msetClearCode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDEFAULT_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `ZCompressorInputStream` constructor reads a [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m‐bit “max code size” [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly from the `.Z` file header [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. It then calls [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Because `memoryLimitInKiB` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefaults to –[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno limit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the runtime unconditionally allocates tables of size `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<< maxCodeSize`. Malicious inputs with `maxCodeSize` up to [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m cause allocations of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbillions of entries, exhausting the heap.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The LZW format [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.Z[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m specification only defines valid code sizes in the range [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits. Any value outside this range indicates either a malformed file or a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeliberate attempt to exhaust memory.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy Overview[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enforce a valid range check on `maxCodeSize` immediately after parsing the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader in `ZCompressorInputStream`.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Define class constants for the minimum and maximum supported code sizes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the parsed `maxCodeSize` falls outside [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMIN_SUPPORTED, MAX_SUPPORTED[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow an `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid LZW max code size: "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This rejects [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe input before any large allocations happen.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve the existing `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call for valid code sizes, so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard `.Z` streams decompress normally.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Implementation Steps[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInputStream.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma`:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Add two new private constants at the top of the class:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final int MIN_CODE_SIZE = DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m typically [0m[1;36m9[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final int MAX_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m per .Z spec[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate the constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m77[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m86[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and immediately after [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracting `maxCodeSize`, insert:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < MIN_CODE_SIZE || maxCodeSize > MAX_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[32m"Invalid LZW max code size: "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize +[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[32m" [0m[32m([0m[32msupported range: "[0m[39m + MIN_CODE_SIZE + [0m[32m"–"[0m[39m + MAX_CODE_SIZE + [0m[32m"[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure this check occurs before any call to `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. No other modifications to external libraries, harness code, or test code are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Document this new check in the Javadoc for `ZCompressorInputStream`, noting [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat code sizes outside [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m are rejected to guard against resource exhaustion.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach directly addresses the unbounded memory allocation by filtering [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout malicious or malformed inputs that specify absurdly large code sizes.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid `.Z` files [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich only use code sizes [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will continue to work [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munmodified.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Throwing an `IOException` is consistent with existing error handling for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvalid formats in `ZCompressorInputStream` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., the magic‐byte checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It does not alter the public API [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno new setters or parameters[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclients of `CompressorStreamFactory` remain unaffected.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By rejecting out‐of‐spec inputs early, we avoid any risk of heap exhaustion [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand remove the need to introduce arbitrary memory caps or new factory defaults.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any non‐conforming `.Z` stream that legitimately uses code sizes outside [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwhich should not exist per specification[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now fail with `IOException`. This [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis acceptable given the format standard.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Developers who purposely raise `memoryLimitInKiB` via a future API could still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequest larger tables, but they would be limited by the format‐compliant [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m‐bit [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcap.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should there be a future requirement to support larger code sizes, the [0m        [2m                [0m
